## 50.0.0 (2021-10-26)

### ⚠ BREAKING CHANGES

- **Pattern:** remove name-based Pattern component
- **PageSingleFeature:** add option for accent eyebrow
- **PageHero:** add short text variation
- **CurriculumCard:** Updated scope to support more content items, added alternative subtitle
- **Flyout:** switch to controlled component
- **Card:** Add color mode to card
- **GridForm:** remove business button
- **progress bar:** reduces size of large variant, creates xl for old size
- release -kit-4.7
- **Modal:** Deprecating Modal component
- Refactor Testimonial and Avatar to Emotion
- **Header:** reroute header upsell for upgrade
- add new gamut-patterns package
- add new dot Pattern and rename old dots to checker
- auto-centered ToolTips (#1614)
- **NotificationList:** Replaced old NotificationList & NotificationListItem w/ upgraded components
- converted ToolTip to Emotion (#1409)
- **ContentContainer:** update responsive padding
- **Card:** Animation Fixes and Gamut migration
- **Alert:** New Visual Identity Alert [GM-119]
- **Banner:** Banner new visual identity [GM-123]
- progress bar theme => variant
- converted ToolTip to Emotion (#1357)
- bumped ESLint packages to latest and added recommended & Jest linting
- **BrandMono:** Remove Roboto Mono in favor of using Suisse
- **Alert:** open cta in new tab by default (#1350)
- **PageHero:** added functionality for PageHero to take images or videos as props
- **Toggle:** refactor to emotion and add focus styles
- replace VisualTheme enum with string type union (#1166)
- used Emotion for Anchor
- add landing page prefooter component (#1185)
- deprecate Button and ButtonBase (#1069)
- **gamut-styles:** deprecate legacy JS color variables (#940)
- Swapped default font family to Apercu (#935)
- **Gamut:** Enable Emotion (#917)
- **Accordion:** Decoupled AccordionArea and AccordionButton (#889)
- **Icons:** Streamline Icon Set Full [GM-30] (#838)
- **GridForm:** Simplified GridForm labels to allow React.ReactNode or be hidden (#844)
- **Gamut:** Removed deprecated color variables (#819)
- Refactor Modal and Overlay components [GM-24] (#806)
- **webpack-config:** Update CSS Loader and move loaders into dependencies (#736)
- **Typography:** Heading Primitives and reconfigured responsive styles (#722)
- moved Logo atom to brand-components (#718)
- **Gamut:** removed deprecated primary, blue, red, and yellow button colors (#714)
- **Gamut:** removed easily replaceable deprecated swatches- colors (#717)
- reorganized stories into Atomic Design and TypeScript (#695)
